folio 1r> # page 1
# text only
# Currier's Language A, hand 1
# There is a key-like sequence in the right margin apparently added after
# the main text was written. Unclear in Petersen copies, but seems to be
# the roman alphabet. It starts at the end of the second line and it
# is not well aligned with the rest of the lines: a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h,
# i,{j is missing}k,{l,m,n are not readable},o,p,q,r
# There is non-Voynich text at bottom of folio: the signature
# of Jacobus de Tepenecz
#  
# At the end of the paragraphs there are further words (right justified)
# as if they were the name of the author in a quotation.
# The space between the paragraph and these "signatures" is marked with a
# {space} comment.
# Next to the end of the 1st. line there is a thick non-Voynich symbol
# resembling an underlined 29 and marked {doodle}
# The 2nd and 3rd paragraphs start with thick non-Voynich symbols. These
# are also marked {doodle}
> 
# folio 1 r.1 ... marks the folio 'f' number 1 'r' reverse or 'v' verse
> 
# The following transcription of the Voynich script uses the EVA encoding:
# EVA mapping

b	󿐈
c	󿐌
d	󿐉

g	󿐋

# herbal
# Currier's language A, hand 1
# Plant ID: uva lupi, aterpa belladonn[a], solatrum d[iv|w]ale, solanum nigrum=morella
#           Ref: Fuchs p.398, Fischer p.17
# Same plant as f102r1[3,2] (Petersen, Stolfi) WHAT? NOT AT ALL!
# Two paragraphs of text, plant cutting through middle
#

folio 53 v.9 󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁

folio 58 r.20 󿐗󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐆󿐆󿐊󿐆󿐗 󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐐󿐚 󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐃󿐔󿐉󿐐[󿐀:?]󿐄
folio 58 r.21 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐗󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐚󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐗

folio 58 v.1 󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐠󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐗󿐡󿐐󿐃 󿐗󿐡󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐚󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁
folio 58 v.2 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐃 {󿐌󿐏󿐰󿐏}󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊,󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐃󿐢󿐗
folio 58 v.3 󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐔[{󿐌󿐢}:󿐢]󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐐󿐚 󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐄
folio 58 v.4 󿐔󿐃,󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃,󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃,󿐐󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚
folio 58 v.5 󿐠󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐠󿐐󿐊,󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗
folio 58 v.6 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐔[󿐃:󿐊] 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃󿐋 󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐗
folio 58 v.7 󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚󿐊 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐢󿐗
folio 58 v.8 󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐃 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐄
folio 58 v.9 󿐊󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁󿐔󿐊 󿐔󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐐󿐚󿐗
folio 58 v.10 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐄 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐊 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐃󿐗
folio 58 v.11 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐣󿐔󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐃 󿐗,󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐉󿐔󿐃󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐊

folio 58 v.12 󿐔󿐃󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐐󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐉󿐗 󿐣󿐔󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐡󿐔󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐌󿐠󿐏󿐗

folio 66r> # page 117
# text only
# Currier's language B
# has 'key-like' sequence
# has non-Voynich writing
# Brumbaugh Yale Lib Gaz p352
# Roe, 3 Sept 93
# Normal text in paragraphs with, to the left, single characters
# (not exactly one per line) and left of that occasional single words.
# The text layout of Mike Roe is not used here.
# Text near the 'dead body' is label, and all other characters
# and words 'scattered'.
#  
# R In the bottom left hand corner, there is a picture of a woman lying down
# R (dead?). To the left of the woman are two circles and a cylinde r. Above
# R her are four words in Voynich text. To the far left are four words in
# R a different hand and a different alphabet. To me they look like:
# R     v
# R Den  mv<illegible>
# R    der
# R In the bottom right hand corner there is a symbol that looks like a number 2
# R on its side.
# Loci: S1 to S15 for the full words at the extreme left,
#       S16 to S49 for the individual characters
#

folio 67r2> # page 121, 124
# astronomical
# General description of page:
# Circular diagram with 12 sectors and 12 moon or planet faces.
# One outer circle in red ink, with 12 pieces of scattered writing in red ink.
# Middle circle is divided in 12 radial sections with short paragraphs.
# Sector nrs are cf. Petersen, first = from 09:00 to 10:00 and further clockwise.
# Inner circle with  8 words around an 8-point star with clouds (?)
# From one of the star point there is a radiating dotted line that runs up
# to the lower part of the middle section.
# Each of the middle sections starts with text, in 7 cases with one "heading",
# which is transcribed as a combination of blocked and scattered loci.
# More inside are 12 labels near moon faces and inside that 8 more words (S loci).
# At NW of the circle there seems to be a line that marks the start of text (?)
#  
# Has 'b' in upper right corner
#  
# Outside ring:

folio 67v2> # page 122
# cosmological
# Roe, 6th September 1993
# Machine-translated from transcription in Bennett notation dated April 1990
# This is plate XX in Newbold, and plate IV in Manly31. Newbold's folio number
# scheme has this as 67 r.
# This is the folio Newbold claimed showed an annular eclipse. See also John
# Manley's 1931 article in Speculum: "Furthermore, I invite the reader to
# examine carefully Plate IV and say whether it bears any resemblance whatever
# to an annular eclipse."
# General description of page:
# There is a large circle centered on the page. Outside this circle, in the
# NE, SE, SW and NW corners, are four smaller circles. In the center of the
# large circle is a square, within which is inscribed another circle, within
# which is a sta r.
# From the square, lines radiate out in the N, S, E and W directions. Lines
# come in towards the square from the perimeter of the large circle in the NE,
# NW, SE and SW direction. Each of these eight lines are terminated with a
# branching broccoli-like structure.
# The small circles in the corners contain between one and four human faces,
# joined by lines.
# There is a "sentence'' of Voynich text above, below, to the left and the
# right of the large circle. The bottom left small circle contains a "word''
# of Voynich text.
#  
# Labels in upper left and right circles

# astronomical
# General description of page:
# A large circle filled with stars, with each with a label
# At the top, within the large circle, is a smaller circle with a moon in

#
folio 70v2> # page 135
# Pisces
#  
# General description of page:
# Three concentric rings of text. In the centre are two fish (the astrological
# symbol for Pisces), two stars, a ``word'' of Voynich text and the word Mars
# in the Roman alphabet. Mars is French for March, Pisces is February 20th to
# March 20th.
#  
# Between the inner ring and the middle ring are ten female(?) figures, each
# beside a barrel and holding a sta r. Between the middle and the outer ring
# are 19 (NOT 20) female figures, each standing in a barrel and holding a star
# Each of the figures in the 29 figures is labelled with a "word" or phrase
# of Voynich text.
#  
# Circular text, locus indications C1 to C3 (outer to inner)
#  
folio 70v2.1 󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐐󿐄 󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐗 󿐗󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆[󿐗:󿐔] 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐌󿐣󿐏 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐊󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐆󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐔 󿐗󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐗 {󿐌@162;󿐏}󿐔 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐐󿐚 󿐐󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐊 󿐌󿐏󿐔 󿐊 󿐔󿐚󿐐[󿐃:󿐁] 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐔󿐊

folio 70v1> # page 136
# Aries (dark)
# Gathering mark 10
# Two concentric circles of text. In the centre is the astrological
# symbol for Aries (dark) eating a plant, word "Abril" in the Roman
# alphabet. Abril is Spanish for April, Aries is March 20th to April 20th.
#

folio 71v> # page 138
# Taurus (light)
#  
# General description of page:
# Three concentric rings of text, locus indications C1 to C3 (outer
# to inner). In the centre is a Taurus feeding from a mange r. Below
# the bull is the word ``May'' in the Roman alphabet. Between the
# inner ring of text and the middle ring are five
# human figures, each in a barrel, holding a star, and labelled with a word
# of Voynich text. One is naked, four are clothed. Between the middle ring
# and the outer ring are 10 human figures, each in a barrel, holding a star,
# and labeled with a word of Voynich text. Two are naked, eight are clothed.
#  
# Newbold calls this folio 79 and he reads the date of the comet 1273.
# The photograph in Newbold is cropped, so part of ring C1 isn't visible.
# There is a gap at 10:00 which could be the start instead of ThP's choice
#  
folio 71 v.1 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐡󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆 󿐐󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗,󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐔 󿐔󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 ???󿐗 ???󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐄 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐗 {󿐌󿐡}󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐚 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐊󿐏󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐢󿐆[󿐆:󿐐]󿐃 󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐃󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚󿐊

folio 72r2> # page 140
# Gemini
# Three rings of circular text, locus indications C1 to C3 (outer
# to inner) and thirty labled nymphs. Inside inner ring the
# emblem of Gemini: two persons holding each other's hands.
# Inside two rings: full circles with labeled nymphs. Five more
# of them are found on top of the outer ring.
# Three nymphs (outer complete ring) are standing on top of
# barrels similar to those of the previous pages.
#

folio 83 r.1 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐚󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐡{󿐌󿐏󿐰}󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐡󿐔󿐚 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗
folio 83 r.2 󿐊󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐊 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐊 󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐔󿐃

folio 83 v.1 󿐡󿐔󿐚󿐉󿐐󿐢󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗

folio 85r2> # page 171
# cosmological
# Currier's language B, hand 3
# sun @ circle divided in 4, 4 human figures.
# 'Four seasons'. Outer and inner circle of text and four
# blocks. Lines in blocks are loci .B1 to .B22 and
# comments are included to show the compass directions.
#

folio 86v4.3 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃,󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐊 󿐝󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐔[󿐊:󿐃],󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆[󿐉:?] 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐆󿐆󿐊 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐃,󿐊󿐏󿐉 󿐊󿐏󿐗,󿐗 󿐊󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐐󿐃,󿐔󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐆󿐊 󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐔 󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐄
folio 86v4.4 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐔{󿐌󿐡}󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐔󿐆󿐊 󿐐󿐀󿐀[󿐃:󿐁] 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐉󿐆󿐊󿐗 󿐉󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐄 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐗 󿐉󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐊 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐔󿐊 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐁 󿐔󿐚 󿐉󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐔 󿐡󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚󿐉󿐗󿐚

folio 86v6.19 󿐡󿐔󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐌󿐠󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃#  
folio 86v6.20 󿐡󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐡󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐌󿐡󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉 󿐝󿐔󿐠󿐔󿐉 󿐔󿐡󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 [󿐔:󿐐]󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃󿐔󿐉󿐗
folio 86v6.21 󿐔󿐃󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐗󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐣󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐄,󿐔󿐉󿐗
folio 86v6.22 󿐚󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐊 󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃󿐔󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐣󿐐{󿐀󿐢󿐏}󿐗 󿐉,󿐐󿐄󿐔󿐄
folio 86v6.23 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐃,󿐐󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚 󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃
folio 86v6.24 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗,󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐗󿐣󿐊󿐏[󿐗:󿐝],󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐗
folio 86v6.25 󿐗󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃,󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐄
folio 86v6.26 󿐊󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐋 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐄
folio 86v6.27 󿐐󿐚󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐃 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐉 󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗,󿐝󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐃󿐐󿐄󿐊󿐏󿐗
folio 86v6.28 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐚󿐔󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐉,󿐗,󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐉󿐗󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐗 󿐉󿐗
folio 86v6.29 󿐉󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐗,󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁#  
folio 86v6.30 󿐡󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐡󿐐󿐃󿐔󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐗󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐃󿐗
folio 86v6.31 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐡󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃,󿐐󿐚 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐄 󿐔󿐃󿐔󿐄
folio 86v6.32 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐊󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐃,󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚 󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐄
folio 86v6.33 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐉󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐚 󿐚󿐉 󿐚󿐔 󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗,󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐋
folio 86v6.34 󿐊󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐚󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐃󿐔 󿐔󿐚 󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁
folio 86v6.35 󿐊󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚 󿐣󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚
folio 86v6.36 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃󿐐󿐚 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁
folio 86v6.37 󿐚󿐊󿐏󿐐󿐃 [󿐔:󿐗]󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐚 󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐆󿐐󿐃 󿐚󿐔
folio 86v6.38 󿐡󿐔󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐣󿐔󿐃󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐣󿐐󿐄
folio 86v6.39 󿐗,󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁,󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐔󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐄
folio 86v6.40 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚 󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐚󿐢󿐗
folio 86v6.41 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐗
folio 86v6.42 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐚󿐣 󿐐󿐚 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁
folio 86v6.43 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐗,󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐁
folio 86v6.44 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐃󿐔󿐚󿐢 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐐󿐚 󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗
folio 86v6.45 󿐡󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐢󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀[󿐔:󿐐]󿐉󿐐󿐄#

folio 86v5.1 󿐡󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐚󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐠󿐗󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐗 󿐗󿐡󿐐󿐃 󿐔 󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐣󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐡󿐗
folio 86v5.2 󿐚󿐔󿐊󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐗󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐚 󿐗󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐄 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐄
folio 86v5.3 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐁
folio 86v5.4 󿐗󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐊󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐐󿐀󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐡󿐗 󿐚󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐄
folio 86v5.5 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃󿐗
folio 86v5.6 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐣󿐗 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐄 󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁#  
folio 86v5.7 󿐡󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐃,󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐠󿐏󿐗
folio 86v5.8 󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐐󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐔󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐔󿐃,󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐣󿐐󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐋

folio 94 v.1 󿐣󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐐󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐁
folio 94 v.2 󿐔󿐚 󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐆󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐗󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐁
folio 94 v.3 󿐗󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐣󿐐󿐄󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐣󿐐󿐄
folio 94 v.4 󿐉󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐗,󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐗#  
folio 94 v.5 󿐣󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐉 󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐃 󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐃,󿐐󿐄
folio 94 v.6 󿐗󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐔 󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐗
folio 94 v.7 󿐣󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁#  
folio 94 v.8 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐡󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐉 󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐡󿐐󿐃,󿐐󿐃
folio 94 v.9 󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁,󿐗 󿐗󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐚 󿐊 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐗
folio 94 v.10 󿐔󿐚 󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐗 󿐣󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐃
folio 94 v.11 󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏{󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐏}󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐗󿐢󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐔󿐃,󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐗
folio 94 v.12 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐣󿐏󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁#

folio 95r1.5 󿐐󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐣󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐗#

folio 95r1.10 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐆󿐡[?:󿐐]󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 [󿐚󿐊:?]
folio 95r1.11 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚 󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐗󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐚󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐢󿐐󿐚#

folio 95v2.2 󿐊󿐔󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐗󿐣󿐗 󿐔󿐚󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐢[󿐐:󿐔]󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗 󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐡󿐗
folio 95v2.3 󿐐󿐃󿐌󿐏󿐗󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐢󿐔󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐉󿐗
folio 95v2.4 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐢󿐗󿐉󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊
folio 95v2.5 󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐊 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁,󿐐󿐃

# Light star, dotted, 8 points, tail
folio 104 v.1 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐔󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐚 󿐆󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐃,󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐉󿐐󿐄
folio 104 v.2 󿐗󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐄󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃,󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐄
folio 104 v.3 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐉 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐚 󿐉[󿐚:󿐔]
folio 104 v.4 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗
folio 104 v.5 󿐉󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐊,󿐐󿐀󿐃󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐󿐚#  
# Light star, 8 points, tail
folio 104 v.6 󿐊󿐔󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐉 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐 󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐡󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐐󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐉󿐗
folio 104 v.7 󿐔 󿐊󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔{󿐌󿐢}󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐔 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐔󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐚#

# Light star, 7 points, tail
folio 106 v.1 󿐠󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐐 󿐚󿐔󿐔󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐃󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐚󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐚󿐗 󿐢󿐐󿐃
folio 106 v.2 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐗,󿐌󿐏󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐐󿐃,󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐔[󿐣:󿐢]󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐔 󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐁,󿐐󿐄󿐌󿐏󿐗

folio 107 v.1 󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐊󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣[󿐔:󿐆]󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗

folio 107 v.9 󿐊󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗,󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐗,󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐣󿐐󿐃,󿐐󿐣󿐗
folio 107 v.10 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗#

# Light star, dotted?, 7 points, tail
folio 112 v.1 󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐃,󿐗 󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐃 󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐊 󿐐󿐄
folio 112 v.2 󿐔󿐐󿐃 󿐔[󿐃:󿐊]󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐊󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐗 󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁
folio 112 v.3 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐃 󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐚 󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐄
folio 112 v.4 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔 󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐗 󿐐󿐄
folio 112 v.5 󿐊󿐐󿐀󿐁 󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐗 󿐉󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐚 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐚󿐉󿐗
folio 112 v.6 󿐊󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 [󿐔:󿐐]󿐚 󿐔󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐢[?:󿐆󿐆]󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐐{󿐀󿐢󿐏}󿐗#  
# Light star, 7 points, tail??
folio 112 v.7 󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐗 󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐆󿐢󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐆󿐆󿐊,󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐉󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐐󿐃󿐗

folio 113 v.1 󿐠󿐔󿐚󿐔󿐃󿐐󿐃󿐔󿐄 󿐔󿐣󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐃 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐗,󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐗 󿐃󿐔󿐚 󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐃 󿐌󿐏[󿐊:󿐃]󿐔󿐄,󿐔󿐢󿐗

# Light star, dotted, 7 points, tail
folio 113 v.7 󿐠󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐊󿐏󿐉,󿐣󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐚󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐚󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐐󿐚󿐐󿐀󿐄 󿐊󿐏󿐔󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐔󿐚 󿐔󿐡󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐀󿐀󿐁 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃,󿐐󿐃,󿐐󿐚 󿐔󿐣󿐆󿐐󿐚
folio 113 v.8 󿐗󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐔󿐉󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐆󿐆󿐔󿐃 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐚󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐔󿐚󿐢󿐐󿐄 󿐌󿐏󿐔󿐢󿐐󿐄 󿐔󿐉󿐐󿐚 󿐊󿐏󿐆󿐌󿐢󿐏󿐗 󿐝󿐔󿐢󿐌󿐏󿐆󿐉󿐗 󿐔󿐣󿐔󿐃 󿐔󿐣󿐐󿐃 󿐣󿐔󿐢󿐗
